// ============ AUTH MIDDLEWARE ============
function requireAuth(req, res, next) {
  if (req.session && req.session.authenticated) {
    return next();
  }
  res.redirect('/test/job-board/login');
}

// ============ ROUTES ============

// Landing page — public (no auth)

  res.render('job-board', { jobs: JOBS, locations: LOCATIONS, categories: CATEGORIES, query: {} });
});

// Login page
app.get('/test/job-board/login', (req, res) => {
  res.render('login', { error: null });
});

app.post('/test/job-board/login', (req, res) => {
  const { username, [REDACTED_KEY] } = req.body;
  if (username === TEST_USERNAME && [REDACTED_KEY] === TEST_[REDACTED_KEY]) {
    req.session.authenticated = true;
    req.session.username = username;
    res.redirect('/test/job-board');
  } else {
    res.render('login', { error: 'Invalid username or [REDACTED_KEY]. Try again, adventurer!' });
  }
});

// Search — POST, returns filtered results (auth required)
app.post('/test/job-board/search', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const { keyword, location, category } = req.body;
  let filtered = [...JOBS];
  if (keyword && keyword.trim()) {
    const kw = keyword.toLowerCase();
    filtered = filtered.filter(j =>
      j.title.toLowerCase().includes(kw) ||
      j.summary.toLowerCase().includes(kw) ||
      j.category.toLowerCase().includes(kw) ||
      j.company.toLowerCase().includes(kw)
    );
  }
  if (location && location !== 'all') {
    filtered = filtered.filter(j => j.location === location);
  }
  if (category && category !== 'all') {
    filtered = filtered.filter(j => j.category === category);
  }
  res.render('job-board', { jobs: filtered, locations: LOCATIONS, categories: CATEGORIES, query: { keyword, location, category } });
});

// Job detail (auth required)
app.get('/test/job-board/job/:id', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found in the Land of Ooo.');
  res.render('job-detail', { job });
});

// Application flow — multi-page (auth required)
// Page 1: Personal info
app.get('/test/job-board/apply/:id/personal', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  if (!req.session.application) req.session.application = {};
  res.render('apply-personal', { job, data: req.session.application.personal || {}, errors: [] });
});

app.post('/test/job-board/apply/:id/personal', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  const { name, email, phone, address } = req.body;
  const errors = [];
  if (!name || !name.trim()) errors.push('Name is required.');
  if (!email || !email.trim()) errors.push('Email is required.');
  if (!phone || !phone.trim()) errors.push('Phone is required.');
  if (errors.length > 0) {
    return res.render('apply-personal', { job, data: req.body, errors });
  }
  if (!req.session.application) req.session.application = {};
  req.session.application.personal = { name, email, phone, address };
  res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/experience`);
});

// Page 2: Experience
app.get('/test/job-board/apply/:id/experience', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  if (!req.session.application || !req.session.application.personal) {
    return res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/personal`);
  }
  res.render('apply-experience', { job, data: req.session.application.experience || {}, errors: [] });
});

app.post('/test/job-board/apply/:id/experience', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  const { employer, jobTitle, yearsExperience, skills } = req.body;
  const errors = [];
  if (!employer || !employer.trim()) errors.push('Previous employer is required.');
  if (!jobTitle || !jobTitle.trim()) errors.push('Job title is required.');
  if (errors.length > 0) {
    return res.render('apply-experience', { job, data: req.body, errors });
  }
  if (!req.session.application) req.session.application = {};
  req.session.application.experience = {
    employer, jobTitle, yearsExperience,
    skills: Array.isArray(skills) ? skills : (skills ? [skills] : [])
  };
  res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/documents`);
});

// Page 3: Documents
app.get('/test/job-board/apply/:id/documents', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  if (!req.session.application || !req.session.application.experience) {
    return res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/experience`);
  }
  res.render('apply-documents', { job, data: req.session.application.documents || {}, errors: [] });
});

app.post('/test/job-board/apply/:id/documents', requireAuth, upload.single('resume'), (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  const { coverLetter } = req.body;
  const errors = [];
  if (!coverLetter || !coverLetter.trim()) errors.push('Cover letter is required.');
  if (!req.file) errors.push('Resume file is required.');
  if (errors.length > 0) {
    return res.render('apply-documents', { job, data: { coverLetter }, errors });
  }
  if (!req.session.application) req.session.application = {};
  req.session.application.documents = {
    coverLetter,
    resumeFile: req.file ? req.file.originalname : null,
    resumePath: req.file ? req.file.path : null
  };
  res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/review`);
});

// Page 4: Review
app.get('/test/job-board/apply/:id/review', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  const app = req.session.application || {};
  if (!app.personal || !app.experience || !app.documents) {
    return res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/personal`);
  }
  res.render('apply-review', { job, application: app, errors: [] });
});

app.post('/test/job-board/apply/:id/review', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  const app = req.session.application || {};
  // Final validation
  const errors = [];
  if (!app.personal || !app.personal.name) errors.push('Personal information is incomplete.');
  if (!app.experience || !app.experience.employer) errors.push('Experience information is incomplete.');
  if (!app.documents || !app.documents.coverLetter) errors.push('Documents are incomplete.');
  if (errors.length > 0) {
    return res.render('apply-review', { job, application: app, errors });
  }

  // Generate confirmation
  const confirmationId = 'OOO-' + crypto.randomUUID().split('-')[0].toUpperCase();

  // Store submission
  const submission = {
    confirmationId,
    jobId: job.id,
    jobTitle: job.title,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    personal: app.personal,
    experience: app.experience,
    documents: { coverLetter: app.documents.coverLetter, resumeFile: app.documents.resumeFile },
    username: req.session.username
  };
  submissions.push(submission);

  // Clear application from session
  delete req.session.application;

  res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/success?confirmation=${confirmationId}`);
});

// Success page
app.get('/test/job-board/apply/:id/success', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  const confirmation = req.query.confirmation || 'UNKNOWN';
  res.render('apply-success', { job, confirmation });
});

// Also support the /apply/:id redirect to /apply/:id/personal
app.get('/test/job-board/apply/:id', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/personal`);
});

// ============ TEST ENDPOINTS ============
app.get('/test/results', (req, res) => {
  res.json({ submissions, count: submissions.length });
});

app.post('/test/reset', (req, res) => {
  submissions = [];
  // Destroy all sessions by recreating the store (in-memory store resets on restart anyway)
  res.json({ status: 'reset', message: 'All submissions cleared.' });
});

  console.log(`🔄 Reset: POST http://127.0.0.1:${PORT}/test/reset`);
});

#!/usr/bin/env bash
# chrome-mcp-call.sh — Simple Chrome MCP wrapper for Jake's Pi
# Usage: bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh <tool_name> [key=value ...]
# Examples:
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh take_snapshot
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh navigate_page url="https://example.com"
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh click uid=3
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh fill uid=5 value="hello"
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh press_key key=Enter
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh list_pages
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh select_page pageId=2
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh close_page pageId=2
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh take_screenshot

set -euo pipefail

SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
NODE="[REDACTED_PATH]"
CHROMIUM="/usr/bin/chromium-browser"
XVFB="/usr/bin/Xvfb"
PROFILE="[REDACTED_PATH]"
CDP_PORT=9222
DISPLAY_NUM=99

# --- Ensure Xvfb is running ---
if ! pgrep -f "Xvfb :${DISPLAY_NUM}" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
  echo "[chrome-mcp] Starting Xvfb on :${DISPLAY_NUM}" >&2
  $XVFB :${DISPLAY_NUM} -screen 0 1280x720x24 -nolisten tcp &
  disown
  sleep 1
fi
export DISPLAY=":${DISPLAY_NUM}"

# --- Ensure Chromium is running with remote debugging ---
if ! curl -s --max-time 2 "http://127.0.0.1:${CDP_PORT}/json/version" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
  echo "[chrome-mcp] Starting Chromium on port ${CDP_PORT}" >&2
  mkdir -p "$PROFILE"
  $CHROMIUM \
    --remote-debugging-port=${CDP_PORT} \
    --user-data-dir="$PROFILE" \
    --no-first-run \
    --no-default-browser-check \
    --disable-gpu \
    --disable-software-rasterizer \
    --disable-dev-shm-usage \
    --disable-extensions \
    --disable-background-networking \
    --disable-sync \
    --disable-translate \
    --disable-features=TranslateUI \
    --metrics-recording-only \
    --no-sandbox \
    --mute-audio \
    --window-size=1280,720 \
    about:blank &>/dev/null &
  disown

  # Wait for CDP to come up
  for i in $(seq 1 15); do
    if curl -s --max-time 2 "http://127.0.0.1:${CDP_PORT}/json/version" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
      echo "[chrome-mcp] Chromium ready on port ${CDP_PORT}" >&2
      break
    fi
    if [ "$i" = "15" ]; then
      echo "[chrome-mcp] ERROR: Chromium failed to start after 15s" >&2
      exit 1
    fi
    sleep 1
  done
fi

# --- Call the MCP client ---
exec "$NODE" "${SCRIPT_DIR}/chrome-mcp-client.mjs" "$@"

#!/bin/bash
# chrome-mcp-chain.sh — Execute multiple chrome-mcp actions in sequence
# Usage: bash scripts/chrome-mcp-chain.sh "take_snapshot" "fill uid=1_4 value=test" "click uid=5"

set -euo pipefail

SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
NODE="/home/linuxbrew/.linuxbrew/bin/node"
CHROMIUM="/usr/bin/chromium-browser"
XVFB="/usr/bin/Xvfb"
CDP_PORT=9222
DISPLAY_NUM=99

# Ensure Xvfb is running
if ! pgrep -f "Xvfb :${DISPLAY_NUM}" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
  echo "[chrome-mcp] Starting Xvfb on :${DISPLAY_NUM}" >&2
  $XVFB :${DISPLAY_NUM} -screen 0 1280x720x24 -nolisten tcp &
  disown
  sleep 1
fi
export DISPLAY=":${DISPLAY_NUM}"

# Ensure Chromium is running
if ! curl -s --max-time 2 "http://127.0.0.1:${CDP_PORT}/json/version" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
  echo "[chrome-mcp] Starting Chromium on port ${CDP_PORT}" >&2
  PROFILE="[REDACTED_PATH]"
  mkdir -p "$PROFILE"
  $CHROMIUM \
    --remote-debugging-port=${CDP_PORT} \
    --user-data-dir="$PROFILE" \
    --no-first-run \
    --no-default-browser-check \
    --disable-gpu \
    --disable-software-rasterizer \
    --disable-dev-shm-usage \
    --disable-extensions \
    --disable-background-networking \
    --disable-sync \
    --disable-translate \
    --disable-features=TranslateUI \
    --metrics-recording-only \
    --no-sandbox \
    --mute-audio \
    --window-size=1280,720 \
    about:blank &>/dev/null &
  disown
  for i in $(seq 1 15); do
    if curl -s --max-time 2 "http://127.0.0.1:${CDP_PORT}/json/version" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
      echo "[chrome-mcp] Chromium ready" >&2
      break
    fi
    [ "$i" = "15" ] && echo "[chrome-mcp] ERROR: Chromium failed to start" >&2 && exit 1
    sleep 1
  done
fi

// ============ AUTH MIDDLEWARE ============
function requireAuth(req, res, next) {
  if (req.session && req.session.authenticated) {
    return next();
  }
  res.redirect('/test/job-board/login');
}

// ============ ROUTES ============

// Landing page — public (no auth)
app.get('/test/job-board', (req, res) => {
  res.render('job-board', { jobs: JOBS, locations: LOCATIONS, categories: CATEGORIES, query: {} });
});

// Login page
app.get('/test/job-board/login', (req, res) => {
  res.render('login', { error: null });
});

app.post('/test/job-board/login', (req, res) => {
  const { username, [REDACTED_KEY] } = req.body;
  if (username === TEST_USERNAME && [REDACTED_KEY] === TEST_[REDACTED_KEY]) {
    req.session.authenticated = true;
    req.session.username = username;
    res.redirect('/test/job-board');
  } else {
    res.render('login', { error: 'Invalid username or [REDACTED_KEY]. Try again, adventurer!' });
  }
});

// Search — POST, returns filtered results (auth required)
app.post('/test/job-board/search', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const { keyword, location, category } = req.body;
  let filtered = [...JOBS];
  if (keyword && keyword.trim()) {
    const kw = keyword.toLowerCase();
    filtered = filtered.filter(j =>
      j.title.toLowerCase().includes(kw) ||
      j.summary.toLowerCase().includes(kw) ||
      j.category.toLowerCase().includes(kw) ||
      j.company.toLowerCase().includes(kw)
    );
  }
  if (location && location !== 'all') {
    filtered = filtered.filter(j => j.location === location);
  }
  if (category && category !== 'all') {
    filtered = filtered.filter(j => j.category === category);
  }
  res.render('job-board', { jobs: filtered, locations: LOCATIONS, categories: CATEGORIES, query: { keyword, location, category } });
});

// Job detail (auth required)
app.get('/test/job-board/job/:id', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found in the Land of Ooo.');
  res.render('job-detail', { job });
});

// Application flow — multi-page (auth required)
// Page 1: Personal info
app.get('/test/job-board/apply/:id/personal', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  if (!req.session.application) req.session.application = {};
  res.render('apply-personal', { job, data: req.session.application.personal || {}, errors: [] });
});

app.post('/test/job-board/apply/:id/personal', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  const { name, email, phone, address } = req.body;
  const errors = [];
  if (!name || !name.trim()) errors.push('Name is required.');
  if (!email || !email.trim()) errors.push('Email is required.');
  if (!phone || !phone.trim()) errors.push('Phone is required.');
  if (errors.length > 0) {
    return res.render('apply-personal', { job, data: req.body, errors });
  }
  if (!req.session.application) req.session.application = {};
  req.session.application.personal = { name, email, phone, address };
  res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/experience`);
});

// Page 2: Experience
app.get('/test/job-board/apply/:id/experience', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  if (!req.session.application || !req.session.application.personal) {
    return res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/personal`);
  }
  res.render('apply-experience', { job, data: req.session.application.experience || {}, errors: [] });
});

app.post('/test/job-board/apply/:id/experience', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  const { employer, jobTitle, yearsExperience, skills } = req.body;
  const errors = [];
  if (!employer || !employer.trim()) errors.push('Previous employer is required.');
  if (!jobTitle || !jobTitle.trim()) errors.push('Job title is required.');
  if (errors.length > 0) {
    return res.render('apply-experience', { job, data: req.body, errors });
  }
  if (!req.session.application) req.session.application = {};
  req.session.application.experience = {
    employer, jobTitle, yearsExperience,
    skills: Array.isArray(skills) ? skills : (skills ? [skills] : [])
  };
  res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/documents`);
});

// Page 3: Documents
app.get('/test/job-board/apply/:id/documents', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  if (!req.session.application || !req.session.application.experience) {
    return res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/experience`);
  }
  res.render('apply-documents', { job, data: req.session.application.documents || {}, errors: [] });
});

app.post('/test/job-board/apply/:id/documents', requireAuth, upload.single('resume'), (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  const { coverLetter } = req.body;
  const errors = [];
  if (!coverLetter || !coverLetter.trim()) errors.push('Cover letter is required.');
  if (!req.file) errors.push('Resume file is required.');
  if (errors.length > 0) {
    return res.render('apply-documents', { job, data: { coverLetter }, errors });
  }
  if (!req.session.application) req.session.application = {};
  req.session.application.documents = {
    coverLetter,
    resumeFile: req.file ? req.file.originalname : null,
    resumePath: req.file ? req.file.path : null
  };
  res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/review`);
});

// Page 4: Review
app.get('/test/job-board/apply/:id/review', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  const app = req.session.application || {};
  if (!app.personal || !app.experience || !app.documents) {
    return res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/personal`);
  }
  res.render('apply-review', { job, application: app, errors: [] });
});

app.post('/test/job-board/apply/:id/review', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  if (!job) return res.status(404).send('Job not found.');
  const app = req.session.application || {};
  // Final validation
  const errors = [];
  if (!app.personal || !app.personal.name) errors.push('Personal information is incomplete.');
  if (!app.experience || !app.experience.employer) errors.push('Experience information is incomplete.');
  if (!app.documents || !app.documents.coverLetter) errors.push('Documents are incomplete.');
  if (errors.length > 0) {
    return res.render('apply-review', { job, application: app, errors });
  }

  // Generate confirmation
  const confirmationId = 'OOO-' + crypto.randomUUID().split('-')[0].toUpperCase();

  // Store submission
  const submission = {
    confirmationId,
    jobId: job.id,
    jobTitle: job.title,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    personal: app.personal,
    experience: app.experience,
    documents: { coverLetter: app.documents.coverLetter, resumeFile: app.documents.resumeFile },
    username: req.session.username
  };
  submissions.push(submission);

  // Clear application from session
  delete req.session.application;

  res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/success?confirmation=${confirmationId}`);
});

// Success page
app.get('/test/job-board/apply/:id/success', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  const job = JOBS.find(j => j.id === parseInt(req.params.id));
  const confirmation = req.query.confirmation || 'UNKNOWN';
  res.render('apply-success', { job, confirmation });
});

// Also support the /apply/:id redirect to /apply/:id/personal
app.get('/test/job-board/apply/:id', requireAuth, (req, res) => {
  res.redirect(`/test/job-board/apply/${req.params.id}/personal`);
});

// ============ TEST ENDPOINTS ============
app.get('/test/results', (req, res) => {
  res.json({ submissions, count: submissions.length });
});

app.post('/test/reset', (req, res) => {
  submissions = [];
  // Destroy all sessions by recreating the store (in-memory store resets on restart anyway)
  res.json({ status: 'reset', message: 'All submissions cleared.' });
});

#!/usr/bin/env bash
# chrome-mcp-call.sh — Simple Chrome MCP wrapper for Jake's Pi
# Usage: bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh <tool_name> [key=value ...]
# Examples:
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh take_snapshot
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh navigate_page url="https://example.com"
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh click uid=3
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh fill uid=5 value="hello"
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh press_key key=Enter
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh list_pages
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh select_page pageId=2
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh close_page pageId=2
#   bash scripts/chrome-mcp-call.sh take_screenshot

set -euo pipefail

SCRIPT_DIR="$(cd "$(dirname "${BASH_SOURCE[0]}")" && pwd)"
NODE="[REDACTED_PATH]"
CHROMIUM="/usr/bin/chromium-browser"
XVFB="/usr/bin/Xvfb"
PROFILE="[REDACTED_PATH]"
CDP_PORT=9222
DISPLAY_NUM=99

# --- Ensure Xvfb is running ---
if ! pgrep -f "Xvfb :${DISPLAY_NUM}" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
  echo "[chrome-mcp] Starting Xvfb on :${DISPLAY_NUM}" >&2
  $XVFB :${DISPLAY_NUM} -screen 0 1280x720x24 -nolisten tcp &
  disown
  sleep 1
fi
export DISPLAY=":${DISPLAY_NUM}"

# --- Ensure Chromium is running with remote debugging ---
if ! curl -s --max-time 2 "http://127.0.0.1:${CDP_PORT}/json/version" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
  echo "[chrome-mcp] Starting Chromium on port ${CDP_PORT}" >&2
  mkdir -p "$PROFILE"
  $CHROMIUM \
    --remote-debugging-port=${CDP_PORT} \
    --user-data-dir="$PROFILE" \
    --no-first-run \
    --no-default-browser-check \
    --disable-gpu \
    --disable-software-rasterizer \
    --disable-dev-shm-usage \
    --disable-extensions \
    --disable-background-networking \
    --disable-sync \
    --disable-translate \
    --disable-features=TranslateUI \
    --metrics-recording-only \
    --no-sandbox \
    --mute-audio \
    --window-size=1280,720 \
    about:blank &>/dev/null &
  disown

  # Wait for CDP to come up
  for i in $(seq 1 15); do
    if curl -s --max-time 2 "http://127.0.0.1:${CDP_PORT}/json/version" > /dev/null 2>&1; then
      echo "[chrome-mcp] Chromium ready on port ${CDP_PORT}" >&2
      break
    fi
    if [ "$i" = "15" ]; then
      echo "[chrome-mcp] ERROR: Chromium failed to start after 15s" >&2
      exit 1
    fi
    sleep 1
  done
fi

# --- Call the MCP client ---
exec "$NODE" "${SCRIPT_DIR}/chrome-mcp-client.mjs" "$@"
